3a1(1): cad kyi rgya mtsho chen po la 'jug pa'i sgra'i ro grags par gyur to// de'i tshe 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor mang po de dag thams cad de lta bu'i sprin dang / chad pa sna
3a2(1): tshogs mthong zhing de ltar chos kyis spu ring ro yang thos par gyur nas/ de dag so so'i yid la mos pa bzhin du/ so so'i lus la rnam pa sna tshogs kyi bsung ba dang / me togs
3a3(1): dang / rin po tsho dang brgyad dang / lha rdzas kyi gos dam pa'i yongs su brgyan par mthong ngo // yang so so'i lag zil gnyis na yid bzhin gyi norang du rin po la che thogs shing / 
3a4(1): yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che de dag re re las kyang rin po che rnam pa sna tshogs char bzhin du 'bad par mthong ngo // gzhan yang nor bu rin po che de dag las 'od zer rnam pa sna tshogs pa ste
3a5(1): 'od zer de dag gi dbang gis sems can de dag so so'i nas phyogs bcu'i chu klung gang gi bye ma snyed kyis sangs rgyas kyis zhing yang mthong ngo // yang 'od zer de dag gi dbang gis
3a6(1): sangs rgyas kyis zhing de dag na de bzhin gshegs pa de re re la yang 'khor mang po tshad med pa'i bsti stang dang bcas te yongs su bskor bar mthong ngo // gzhan yang 'od zer de'i
3a7(1): dbang gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag na sems can gad kyis gzir ba thams cad kyang/ 'od zer de dag gis reg ma thag tu nad kyis bsngal dang bral bar gyur to// 
3a8(1): bang gas dpal thug pa dang / btson du bzung zhing bcings po dag kyang 'od zer de dag gis reg ma thag tu de las yongs su thar bar gyur to// gang lus dang ngag dang yid mi bde
3b1(1): bang spyong bdags ngas 'das padag kyang 'a de dbang gis shi tu mang shing rnam par dag par byar togang bkres shi skos padag kyang 'byungs zhing ngosas par gyur / 
3b2(1): bdang bcid parnab pa tshogs kyis na mongs padag kyang / 'od kyis reg ma thag du sdug bsngal dang zal dur gyur to// gang bag dang / rim paci'i rgya dang / 
3b3(1): ring rdzas kyis bkred cing 'phongs padag kyang bsams pa bzhi du byor zhing ldan par gyur te/ sems can gang srog btsod pa la dasa' nang thom pa la/ dga' ching mos pa nas
3b4(1): lta ba'i bar du dga' ning pos bdag kyang / 'od zer des reg ma thag tu srog gcod pa yongs su spang ba la dga' zhing mos pa nas log par lta ba'i bar du yongs su spong ba la dga'
3b5(1): thos par gyur to// sems can gang 'dod pa mi snyed pa rnam pa sna tshogs kyis sdug bsngal bar gyur pa dag kyang 'od zer des res ma thag du ji ltar de bzhin du/ rnyed
3b6(1): pa gzhan yang 'ong zer de'i dbang gis sangs rgyas kyis ning thams cad kyi semaHna sdug bsngal gyis gdungs pa de dag thams tsabazhinas
6a1(1): na rnal mo snar nas/ mi gleng bzhin du tshugs su ba mtshan gang bgis mchog
6a2(1): byams pa'i rjegs kyis blam la bskyog/ sa chen sar me shin tu bzod/ shes pa zo ba'i sems kun pas/ mnapas// sangs rgyas kun gyi zhing dang
6a3(1): brgyan bde 'i byams dang skyeng rje yas// rgyal ba'i shing kun rab tu 'grangs// sed pe dridra ba kran pa / yang dag ji bzhin 'de bar gnas// yongs su
6a4(1): dag pa'i zhing srad nas// rtog pa can gyi sems can dgrol// rnyog pa'i ning der dam bcas te// ngan 'gro'i sems can smin par mdzad// yang dag brtan pa'i
6a5(1): bayis// ring mo zhig granas dka' thu baspyad// yun rings dka' thu baspyad pa dag/ mos nas 'jigs pa'i sems kyang skye// sbyin pa tshul khrims bzod pa dang / 
6a6(1): btsun zlas sam ga sashes rab 'byor// sangs rgyas byung chu ba sems dang/ chang na pa thos bsnyen par mchog/ nan ma byung ma
6a7(1): 'gres ni min pachi kun las bsngal/ sos kyi bo gzhan gyi byer// sras srog mchags mngan btung // yang dag dam pa'i chos tshul nang // shudadang rus pa
6a8(1): yang du babang / bdag gi de bgran pata nas//  rnams 'khrugs car dgos/ so so'i sung mang po'i phyir/ tshom dra gco pa partson// da
6b1(1): bodrug rnams rab skams nas// 'dod pa thams cad ring du spangs// 'dras byas mi rtag sdug bsngal te// bdag med stong pa nyid du rtogs// sdug bsngal las kur skye ba yi/ 
6b2(1): rgyu ni 'dod chags sred pa'o// de phyir dbang po drug pas sngar// 'dod chags yongs su bcad par bya// sems gnas pa'i khams tu// rtag par thugs rje chen pos
6b3(1): gnas/ byang chub mchog tu sangs rgyas kyang // sngon gyi smon lam kun mi gtong // sems can gang zhig sdug bsngal gyis// rnam par gzir bdag gzigs na/ shin
6b4(1): tu'abab pa'i brtson 'grus kyis// de la sgrol phyir rab tu brtson// sbyin pa tshul khrims bzod brtson 'grus// bsam gtan shes rab kun bsgoms nas// ji ltar ma ni bu
6b5(1): gcig la/ byams pa'i sems kyis// gso ba bzhin// sngon yang sems can rigs kun// rtag tu byams pa'i thugs bskyed pas// de'i myur du sangs rgyas nas// 
6b6(1): tshad med pa yi 'khor rnams sgrol// ji tsam byang chub spyod bsgoms pa// sems can don du ma 'arngos med// de bas sems can thams cad la// pha rol tu phyin pa drug mi gtong
6b7(1): rtag du dus ngan 'jam 'tsho// bla med byang chub bsgrub bskam nas// da yang dus ngan 'gyu 'i tshe// tha med byang chub rnga mngon sangs rgyas// ngan par lta ba'i lha klu'i mo// gnod sbyin dag
6b8(1): ni kun 'bul te// the tshom gcod cing bder bkod pa// rdo rje la ngu'i lam la'o// tshad med pa yi sde bo dag/ byang chung mchog su lung yang son// mchod 'os 'dren pa'i gcor gyur / 
7a1(1): mchog gi bsod nams ning dra gyur/ dben med pa'i bcom ldan 'das// byams pas 'gro ba kun la sto// chang med grags chen po las/ 
7a2(1): phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten yongs su khyab// de bas byang chub sems dpa' rnams// bdag gi don du bskung ba'i phyir// kun nas lhan cig 'dir 'dus nas// drung ba chen po'i sngun sngar
7a3(1): lpags// rnam pa'i chos rnams thos nas ni// rab tu dga' ba'i sems skyes nas// lhag par yang dge btsun pa skyed de// byang chub stod sa la nan tan 'gyid// rnam par 'dren pa'i chos
7a4(1): kyi mthus// thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgyangs// de bas deng 'dir 'dren khyod kyis// bskrad pa'i 'khor ni sngon ma byung // gnod sbyin khri phrag bcu gsum sbed// rtag tu sha za'i khrag
7a5(1): 'azung ba// thams cad sdig pa'i las btang nas/ byang chub chen por 'bab cing gzhal// kha cig khyad par gzugs mchog dang // 'bo ba ting 'dzin yang dgazong / 
7a6(1): lagacig pags kun pad nas// 'jig mchog ga dgra bcom gyur// kha gcig rgyud med bzhi sgoms shing // khag cig bsrung bzhi la gnas// kha kra cig
7a7(1): ga pa khagacig mthu pa yod la gas/ ga ga na 'ag nga dun/ lag tsug shes rab ga dang ldan// kha gcigaman
7a8(1): la gnas// dekun 'dren pas byin gyis brlabs// bcom ldan 'das gzi' brjid chen po'i mthus// bdud kyi 'khor rnams bcom nas su// rnam pa dgu bcu rtsa lnga la/ 
7b1(1): mu stegs can gyi rigs kun btul// sems can dmyal ba byol song dang // yi dgas lnga min rgyud kun bcom// bde bas sems can bde ba rnams// thams cad
7b2(1): rgyal ba'i spyan sngar lhags// nad dang mtshon gyis 'jigs pa dang // mu ges 'jigs pa 'du 'dir bcil// sems can mngoms shing thob dang // yang dga' ma ni skor bslal// 
7b3(1): nyon mongs myos shing 'khrug pa dag/ thams cad zhi ba'i lam la bkod// bdag gis bya ba kun spangs te// lpags nas bcom ldan zhabs la thug/ dag tu med pa'i zhing
7b4(1): rnams na/ bcom ldan da ltar bzhugs pa rnams// thams cad khyod la kun sngags pas// thos nas thams cad 'ani ru lhags// thams cad mkhyen rgya mtsho yi// 
7b5(1): yang dag yon tan tshangs ma mchis// sems can mang po'i don mdzad pa// mos pa'i sems kyis phyag 'tshal lo// tshad med bsod nas rdzogs bgyis pas// bcom ldan zhabs la
7b6(1): phyag 'tshal gyur// tshad med bskul ba'i bar du yang // mchod pa mang pos mchod par shog/ bdag kyang bcom ldan ji bzhin du/ de lta bu'i ying bzhin dam bcas// rtog pa
7b7(1): can gyi 'jig rten 'dir// tha med byang chub thob par shog/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sa'i snying pos tshigs su bcad pa/ dam pa 'di dag gis bcom ldan
7b8(1): 'das la mngon par bstod nas/ 'khor dang bcas te gzhan yang lha rdzas kyi bsra dang / me tog dang / rnam pa sna tshogs kyi rin po che'i rgyan tshad med pa snyed kyis/ bcom
8a1(1): ldan 'das la mngon par gtor nas// steng gi bar snang la rin po che'i gdugs su gyur te dam pa'i chos mnyan pa'i phyir/ bcom ldan 'das kyi
8a2(1): spyan sngar ci yang mi smra bar 'dug go// de'i tshe 'khor gyis dkyil 'khor der 'dus pa'i 'khor thams cad kyis byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sa'i snying po mthong nas ngo mtshar rmad du
8a3(1): gyur te/ soso nas rnam pa sna tshogs kyi lha rdzas kyi spos dang / me tog rin po che'i rgyan dang / na bza' dang / rgyal mtshan dang / bdun dang / gdugs la sogs paphral te/ byang
8a4(1): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sa'i snying pol mchod pa byas nas// 'di skad ces smras so// bdag cag gis skyed pa rab tu rnyed do// bcom ldan 'das kyis byin gyi brlabs
8a5(1): bris mngon gsum du/ skyes bu chen po khyod mthong nas/ bsti stang dang bcas te mchod pa chen po byas par gyur to/ zhes smra'o// de nas 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de'i nang na byang chung sems dpa
8a6(1): sems dpa' chen po rigs par the tshom 'dri zhes byang zhig 'du ga nyan las langs nas/ gos chags bcos te phrag pa byung nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas/ 
8a7(1): bras mo g.yas pa'i glengs la 'dugs te/ bcom ldan 'das gang na ba der logs su thal mo sbyar nas bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das rigs kyi tha
8a8(1): 'degad nas mchis// gnas pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ning der 'di nas ri srid cig mchis/ yon can dang dge pa'i drang tsam zhig dang ldan na/ bcom ldan 'das kyis ston pa rnam par tshogs kyis badza
8b1(1): laphyir yang bcom ldan 'das kyis yon tan gyi rgya mtsho bsam gyis mi khyab pa la mngon par bstod par gyur/ bdag gis sngon ma mthong bas/ ngo char du gyur na/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bdag cag la bshad
8b2(1): drugasol/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal ba/ rigs kyi bu thong shig/ skyes bu chen po 'dri'i yon tan dang dge ba'i rtsa ba'i tsam pa de'i 'jig rten du bcas brgya dang / mi gakhor thams cad kyis
8b3(1): rtogs par nus pa ma yin no// gal te de bzhin gshegs pas skyes bu de'i yon tan dang dge ba'i rtsa ba rgyas par bshad na/ 'jig rten du bcas pa lha dang mi thams cad kyis mgo rmongs te yid
8b4(1): mchis par 'gyur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rigs par the tshom 'dri bas yang gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das bdag cag la thugs brtse ba'i slad bshad du gsol// bcom ldan
8b5(1): 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ legs par shin tu nyon la yid la bzung shig dang / ngas khyod la phyogs tsam zhig bshad par bya'o// 'di ltar skyes bu chen po de yon tan gyi khyad pa
8b6(1): tshad med bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan no// 'di lta ste dnga' bar 'gro ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par bde bar gnas pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod yul yang shin tu rtogs par
8b7(1): 'jug go// mi skye ba'i chos kyi bzod pa'i khyad par yang thob pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dbang du gyur pa'o// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi sa la bzod pa thob pa'o// 
8b8(1): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o// sem seng ge rab tu sgyings pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi ting nge 'dzin la yang shin tu gnas pa'o// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes
9a1(1): kyi ril yang rab tu 'dzeg pa'o// ru stegs can dngabs kyi rgol ba thams cad shin// choms pasre/ sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba
9a2(1): phyir sangs rgyas kyi zhing ji zhed pa thams cad du de nas par byed do// skyes bu chen po ji ltar gnas pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams kyang de bzhin du gnas te/ gang ting nge 'dzin rnams kyi
9a3(1): tshad med pa'i yon tan gyi khyad par bskyed par gyur pas/ gdul ba'i sems can myed pa dag yongs su smin par byed do// skyes bu chen po de ji ltar gnas pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyis
9a4(1): zhing rnams kyang de bzhin du gyur te/ lag te ye shes mngon par skyes pa zhes bya'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs na/ ting nge 'dzin de'i mthus sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na gnas pa'i
9a5(1): sems can thams cad rathun par ting nge 'dzin rnams kyi spyod yul kun mthong bar 'gyur ro// de ji ltar gnas pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams kyang de bzhin du 'gyur te/ gal te
9a6(1): rangag tu med pa'i ye shes dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs na/ ting nge 'dzin de'i mthus sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na gnas pa'i sems can thams cad kyis nus
9a7(1): babazhin du tshad med pa'i mchod pa'i yo byad dam pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de la na snang dang bcas pasu mchod par 'gyur ro// de'i sgrar gnas pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing
9a8(1): rnams kyang de bzhin du 'gyur te/ gal te rnam par dag pa'i ye shes dran sum tshogs pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs na/ ting nge lachen de'i mthus sangs rgyas kyi ning
9b1(1): de dag na gnas pa'i sems can thams cad kyis mthun par 'dod pa'i spyod yul gyi nyes pa'i skyon tshad med pa mthong nas sems rnam par dag par 'gyur ro// de ji skar gnas pa bzhin du sangs
9b2(1): rgyas kyi zhing rnams kyang de bzhin du 'gyur te/ gal te khrel ba dang ngo tsha dang / ldan pa'i ye shes shes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs na/ ting nge 'dzin de'i mthus sangs rgyas
9b3(1): kye zhing de dag na gnas pa'i sems can thams cad lhag pa'i 'dzem pa dang / ngo tsha ba dang ldan zhing sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos dang yongs su dral nas bas sa mang mi nyams par 'gyur ro// 
9b4(1): de ji ltar gnas pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams kyang de bzhin du 'gyur te/ gal te theg pa thams cad dang ldan pa gsal ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs na/ 
9b5(1): sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag na gnas pa'i sems can thams cad thabs mkhas pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi mig gi mngon par shes pa dang sngon gyi gnas dran pa'i mngon par shes pa dang / 'chi 'pho
9b6(1): dang skye bar mngon par shes pa dang / 'jig rten 'di dang 'jig rten pha rol gyi rgyu dang 'bras bu mngon par rtogs par 'gyur ro// de ji ltar gnas pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams
9b7(1): kyang de bzhin du 'gyur te/ gal te mya ngan med pa mngon par shes pas rig pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms zhugs na/ ting nge 'dzin de'i mthus sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag na
9b8(1): gnas pa'i sems can thams cad mya ngan dang yi mug dang / rmugs pa thams cad dang bral bar 'gyur ro// de ji ltar gnas pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams kyang de bzhin du gyur te/ gal te mngon par
10a1(1): shes pa'i khyad par dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs par sangs rgyas kyi ning de dag na gnas pa'i sems can thams cad thabs mkhas pa'i mngon par shes
10a2(1): bdang ldan par 'gyur ro// de ji ltar gnas pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zing rnams kyang de bzhin du 'gyur te/ gal te 'jig rten kun tu snang ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs na/ ting nge 'gro
10a3(1): de'i mthus phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad mun pa dang bral te/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na gnas pa thams cad kyang phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi ning de kun mngon gsum du mthong bar
10a4(1): 'gyur ro// de'i ltar gnas pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi ning rnams dang de bzhin du 'gyur te/ gal te sangs rgyas kyi sngon ma zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs na ting nge 'dzin de'i
10a5(1): mthus sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag na gnas pa'i sems can thams cad log par ldang yongs su spangs nas dkon mchog gsum la sbyangs su 'gro ra 'gyur ro// dede sar gnas
10a6(1): dusangs rgyas kyi gang de sang du bzhin du 'gyur/ rgyal tho rdo rje'i 'od ces byu 'i ti dzin ma snyoms par zugs na/ nga nge 'dzin de mthums sa rgyas kyi ning ga
10a7(1): khor yub dang / 'ad na chen po dang / ro bstan po dang / rim yin da'i gnan lung ba dang / lung dran dang / nga dza nga/ bsebs dadu/ dpa/ 
10a8(1): che mdang/ bar/ shing ri papa rnams cad ming ngo // sas rgyas kyi shing dan sa mdzangan par gdags par drug dang/ gtsun pan ma drangs pa dang / me 'phrog dang / 
10b1(1): d+hong+ga dang / rims na dA dang / lus ngan pa dang / nam nus pa dang / rdul dang / dri ma dang / mi gtsang ba'i nyal nyi la thams cad kyang ni ning med par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas
10b2(1): kyi zhing yang lag thil bzhin du mnyam zhing bkra shis pa rnaMs pa sna tshogs rang byung ba dang / rnam par dag par 'gyur ba dang / phul du 'gyur ba dang / dam par 'gyur ba dang / mtshan
10b3(1): bzang po du mas yongs su brgyan par 'gyur ro// de ji ltar gnas pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams kyang de bzhin du 'gyur te/ gal te ye shes kyi stobs 'dral dka' nga zhes bya
10b4(1): ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs na/ ting nge 'dzin de'i mthus sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na nas pa'i bdud kyi rgyal po 'khor dang bcas te/ thams cad 'jigs skra gnas dkon mcho
10b5(1): gsum la skyabs su 'gro bar 'gyur ro// de ji ltar gnas pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams kyang de bzhin du 'gyur te/ gal te klog gi 'od zer ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la
10b6(1): snyoms par zhugs na ting nge 'dzin de'i mthus sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams de bzhin du 'gyur te/ gal te de dag na gnas pa'i sems can thams cad 'jig rten pha rol gyi 'jigs pa dang
10b7(1): bral zhing chos kyis spo bar 'gyur ro// de ji ltar gnas pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams kyang de bzhin 'gyur te/ gal te mchog dam pa'i cha ro dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge
10b8(1): 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs na ting nge 'dzin de'i mthus sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na gnas pa'i sems can thams cad bsam pa bzhin du bas dang skom gyis tshim par 'gyur ro// de ji lta gnas
21a1(1): 'byung brkyen po slong dbang dge 'grusangs/ ngan par 'grong skyong du dge dung gsungs sdig pa'i ngag rnabs sbyong ba'ang dge
21a2(1): re ba rdzogs par byed pa dge ba'i ra gsungs/ lo tog smin par byed pa'am dge bar gsungs/ sangs rgyas kun gyis dge bar gsungs pa 'di/ de bzhin gshegs pa kan gyis byin brlang
21a3(1): ga dge bar gsungs 'dis byang chub sems dpa' rnams/ byin gyis rdong mdzad rjes su yi rang ngo // som ldan 'das de ltar me rgya dang ldan pa dang // bkra shis kyi 'od snang ba dang / thos pa
21a4(1): 'dzin pa'i rigs sngags chen po gzungs kyi tshig 'di ni/ bdag gis 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rgya thung gna'i khyimartse de la bsnyen bkur bgyis pas thos so// bzangs 'di na rnam par / 
21a5(1): ba chos thams cad 'phel zhing skye bar bgyid pan/ de bzhin du rgyas pa'i long skyod pa'i so d+ya thams cad kyibar du 'phel zhing skye bar bgyid do// bgran pabacom ldan 'das gzungs 'dzin dupo
21a6(1): ban+de las sgrol bar byed do// bcom ldan 'das kyi kyi gnas su gyung ba dge slong ngang / dge m+ba dang / dge bsnyen ma dang / dge bsnyen ma la sogs pa'i dmigs pa phel bar dbyi nga nas/ 
21a7(1): bzhin du rgyas pa'i tshe ba'i yo thams cad kyi bangar drang bal zhing skye bar bgyid do// gzungs 'di ni bcom ldan 'das kyi 'phags da'i gsung rab bdud rtsil du yongs su rgyas pa dang / dz+nyAn
21a8(1): gnas shing khams gsum gyi sems can thams cad la phan dang / bdeng 'don du 'gyur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos 'i snying ngos thos pa 'dzin pa'i rigs
21b1(1): sngags chen po dang / gzungs kyi tshig 'di sbas pa dang / ri khal de la rab tu g.yos nas lha'i rol mo byed khrug khrig kyang ma dkrol bar rang 'khrol te/ wa'i spos dang / me tog dang /
